Section 2RURAL DEVELOPMENT AND PANCHAYAT RAJ DEPARTMENTA Government Order and Notification were issued for the restructuring and upgradation of the Harur Town Panchayat—by merging with it two Village Panchayats situated within the Harur Panchayat Union in Dharmapuri District—into a new Municipal Council. Accordingly, an Order is hereby issued, and a Notification is published in accordance with Section 15, Sub-section (4)(i) of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21/1994), for the restructuring of rural local bodies by excluding the two aforementioned Village Panchayats from the Harur Panchayat Union.Rural Development and Panchayat Raj DepartmentNotification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(w)/2026,--G.O.Ms.No. 71, Rural Development and Panchayat [Para-2(1)] Department, dated 13th March 2026.19113-03-2026Part II - Section 2Notifications or Orders of interest to a Section of the public issued by Secretariat DepartmentsA Government Order and Notification were issued for the upgradation and restructuring of Namakkal Municipality into the Namakkal Municipal Corporation, by integrating 12 Village Panchayats drawn from the Erumapatti, Mohanur, Puduchatram, and Namakkal Panchayat Unions within Namakkal District. Consequently, an Order and Notification are hereby issued—in accordance with Section 15, Sub-section (4)(i) of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21/1994)—effecting the restructuring of Rural Local Bodies by excluding the said 12 Village Panchayats situated within the Erumapatti, Mohanur, Puduchatram, and Namakkal Panchayat Unions.Rural Development and Panchayat Raj DepartmentNotificaton No. II(2)/RDPR/220(v-1)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/ 220(v-2)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(v-3)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(v-4)/2026.--G.O. Ms. No. 70, Rural Development and Panchayat [Para-2(1)] Department, dated 13th March 2026.19013-03-2026Part II - Section 2Notifications or Orders of interest to a Section of the public issued by Secretariat DepartmentsA Government Order and Notification were issued to upgrade and restructure the Pudukkottai Municipality into the Pudukkottai Municipal Corporation by fully integrating 8 Village Panchayats—and partially integrating 3 Village Panchayats—from the Thiruvarankulam, Pudukkottai, Annavasal, and Arimalam Panchayat Unions within the Pudukkottai District. Consequently, an Order and Notification are hereby issued, in accordance with Section 15, Sub-section (4)(i) of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21/1994), to restructure the Rural Local Bodies by removing—fully in the case of 8 Village Panchayats and partially in the case of 3 Village Panchayats—those entities situated within the Thiruvarankulam, Pudukkottai, Annavasal, and Arimalam Panchayat Unions.Rural Development and Panchayat Raj DepartmentNotification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(u-1)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(u-2)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(u-3)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(u-4)/2026.--G.O. No. 221]	
CHENNAI, MONDAY, APRIL 20,  2026	  
	
Chithirai 7, Parabhava, Thiruvalluvar Aandu–2057
VI-1 Ex. (221)
TAMIL NADU 
GOVERNMENT GAZETTE 
EXTRAORDINARY	
PUBLISHED BY AUTHORITY
THE COMMISSIONER OF LAND ADMINISTRATION, CHEPAUK, CHENNAI-600 005.
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM C
[See Rule 7]
NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION (1) OF SECTION 3 OF THE TAMIL NADU ACQUISITION OF  
LAND FOR INDUSTRIAL PURPOSES ACT, 1997
(CLA-TID/2026/32/01/01/0001)
No. VI(1)/244(a-1)/2026.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO - Northern Rail Connectivity and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land 
for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 25.5485 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
TIDCO -Northern Rail Connectivity.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), unit, 
56A, Abul Kalam Azad Street, Ariyanvoyal, Minjur, Ponneri Taluk, Tiruvallur which may be inspected on any day 
during office hours.
[ 1 ]

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
(CLA-TID/2026/30/01/03/0001)
No. VI(1)/244(a-2)/2026.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO - Multi Modal Logistics Park Railway Connectivity and it having already been 
decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or 
managed by the Managing Director. TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 11.0449 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
TIDCO - Multi Modal Logistics Park Railway Connectivity.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), unit 
Tiruvallur  which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION(1) OF SECTION 3 OF THE TAMIL NADU ACQUISITION OF LANDS FOR 
INDUSTRIAL PURPOSES ACT, 1997 READ WITH THE TAMIL NADU LAND ACQUISITION LAWS (REVIVAL 
OF OPERATION, AMENDMENT AND VALIDATION) ACT, 2019
(CLA-SIP/2026/75/01/01/0001)
No. VI(1)/244(a-3)/2026.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT MARUKALKURICHI INDUSTRIAL PARK and it having already been 
decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or 
managed by the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule 
below measuring an extent of 11.1600 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, 
for SIPCOT - SIPCOT MARUKALKURICHI INDUSTRIAL PARK.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tirunelveli and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit, Tirunelveli which may be inspected on any day during office hours.
The Schedule
Tirunelveli District, Nanguneri Taluk, Marukalkurichi Village.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
27
(CLA-SIP/2026/75/03/01/0001)
No. VI(1)/244(a-4)/2026.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT MARUKALKURICHI INDUSTRIAL PARK and it having already been 
decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or 
managed by the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule 
below measuring an extent of 11.0850 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, 
for SIPCOT - SIPCOT MARUKALKURICHI INDUSTRIAL PARK.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tirunelveli and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit, 
Tirunelveli which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule 
below measuring an extent of 21.6150 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, 
for SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvannamalai and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit, 
Tiruvannamalai which may be inspected on any day during office hours.
